It can be seen from Tables above that:
(1) Over 90% of the respondents were in favour of construction of the espressway
and most respondents held that it will be beneficial to the State. collectives and the
private persons.
-  (2) Over 69% of the respondents agree to obey land acquisition. resettlement, and
compensation: about one third of the respondents have some understanding the road
land acquisition. resettlement and compensation policies, or only knew a little.
(3) Most of the respondents understand the impacts of noise and dusts caused by
hiohway construction and recommended some mitigation measures.
(4) There were a few respondents who didn' t give their answers to some options
and a lot of people didn' t know their relationships with project construction and
reiated policies, and were not clear about the adverse impacts on environment along
139



the road caused by construction and operation. Therefore, it is necessary to enhance
publicity and information release.
8.2 Public Opinions and Suggestions
8.2.1 From individual persons
(1) To build the proposed expressway as soon as possible and to open to traffic as
early as possible.
(2) To provide enough underpasses and overpasses for the convenience of local
people on both sides of the expressway.
(3) The most directly influenced people along the expressway are farmers, who
hope that after the land acquisition, the land compensation should be carried out as
soon as possible and strictly in accordance with the policy to avoid deduction.
(4) The compensation for the resettlement should be carried out in time in
accordance with policies and family conditions, with the living standard after the
resettlement not lower than before.
(5) Noise. tail gas and dust will have some impact on people' s living, but are
within the acceptable scope. The mitigation measures proposed in the EIA are
acceptable.
The above opinions and suggestions have been reflected in the design.
resettlement and assessment documents.
8.2.2 Opinions and suggestions from organizations
(1) They support the construction of the proposed expressway and believe that it
will be beneficial to promoting the economic development in Jiangxi province and to
improving people' s living standards.
(2) Agree with the alignment of the proposed expressway. The Sanjiang town
government hopes to build an auxiliarv bridge besides the Shangyoujiang bridge to
make people convenient to cross the river and to enter into the expresswav.
(3) The negative impacts caused by the highway such as dust. tail gas. traffic
noise. should be mitigated bv some measures such as greening. diversion from
villages, removal and resettlement and setting of soundproof facilities.
(4) It is recommended that in the design and construction stage. it is important to
make close contact with local in designing culverts. bridges and passagewavs.
Compensation money should be in time and in full amount and local surplus labor
force should be hired as much as possible for construction.
The above opinions and suggestions have been reflected in the design resettlement
and assessment documents.
8.3 Information Disclosures and Feedback
(l) Television. broadcasting. newspaper and bulletin should be used to release
information to the public regarding the significance, alignment. resettlement and
140



environmental protection for this project. The World Bank Loan Project office of
JPCD released the bulletin concerning the environmental and resettlement in
.Nanchang Evening, Jingangshan Dailv and Ganzhou Daily dated Oct. 1 0- 11 (Refer to
Annex IV). Relevant inforrnation will be released in the above-mentioned newspapers
in the future.
(2) All the environmental documents such as the EIA. EAP, and El Summary
have been exposed to the public. The Owner has put all environmental documents in
the Reference Room of Taihe county, Wan' an county, Suichuang county and
Ganzhou city. A complete set of environmental documents have been available in the
resettlement offices, besides, the library place and complaint telephone number has
been released in the newspaper. In this case. the public can have access to the related
information not through governmental organizations.
(3) The Owner will set up EP complaint telephone in each level of the
resettlement office, gathering and recording the public' s complaint on environmental
protection. Upon receiving the complaint, the Owner will come to site to solve it
along with local EP bureaus within 48 hours.
(4) In accordance with the environment protection measures specified in the EIA
reports. Jiangxi Provincial Expressway Administration will carry out tracking survey
in each phase as design. construction and operation in the aspects of impact survey on
the people along line. public opinions on the sound barrier. etc.
A random check will be carried out by Jiangxi Provincial Environmental
Protection Bureau to ensure the measures be in place. such as whether Zhuhu school
has been removed, whether the sound barrier for Mashuang school has been built. etc.
8.4 Summary of Pubic Participation
The Owner and design unit attaches great importance to the public opinion. which
have been taken into account in the road design. such as to build an auxiliarv bridge
on both sides of the Shangyoujiang bridge. to build one interchange for each county.
to compare a number of alternative schemes..
As for the environmental concerns caused by the project. the assessment and
design units have proposed corresponding protection measures such as to remove
Zhuhu primarv school. to build sound barriers in Mashuang school. to install
soundproof windows. which.have been agreed by the influenced people.
During its preliminary preparation and design, full consultation and exchange
have been made with local governments. social associations and the public: and the
public opinions have been fully exemplified in the selection of alignment. setting of
interchange and connecting roads. environmental protection and resettlement.
Therefore this project has received wide support from the public.
141



Chapter 9 Assessment Conclusions
9.1 Ecological Environment (including soil erosion)
(1) The ecological environment along the proposed highway assessment area is
good. The main line will take up a total land surface of 11,218.8 mu, including paddy
field, dry land, pond, woodland and wasteland. Construction of this highway will
cause some economic loss for agricultural production, but will not produce significant
impact on the pattem of land distribution and vegetation.
(2) There will be some changes in local terrain and landform owing to the
cutting/filling of earth/stone during road subgrade construction, however, by taking
corresponding engineering protection measures in design, construction and operation
stages of the highway, such adverse impacts in vegetation disruption, land utilization
and farmland change can be minimized.
(3) Investigation shows that there is no wild life reservation area along the
proposed highway. nor is there any precious and endangered animals and plants. Due
to the engineering work. some trees. fruit trees. flowers. bush and crops will be cut.
buried and tramped. affecting some small animal who live on plants and reside on it.
But the above negative impact might be mitigated and compensated for to some extent
by greening measures.
(4) During the construction stage and the initial operation stage. certain amount of
soil erosion will happen owing to the cutting/filling of slopes. The forecast shows that
the soil erosion will reach 29985.075-65523.16 ton/vear if there is no protection
measures at all: but because the protection engineering and the main body engineering
will be simultaneously designed. constructed. completed and accepted. therefore the
actual soil erosion will be far less than the forecasted value. In addition,
implementation of greening measures will recover apart of the vegetation and reduce
the soil erosion in slopes.
9.2 Water Environment
(1) Construction and operation of the large and extra-large bridges will have a
relatively small impact on the water body.
(2) If discharged casuallk. the sew-age from construction camp may have negative
impact on the surrounding environment. Septic tank will be set up at the construction
camp to treat the sewage before it is discharged.
(3) The proposed highway will not exert big impact on the water canals, ponds.
and agricultural irrigation system.
(4) Pollutants in the pavement run-off mainlv are SS and a small amount of
petroleum. mostly occurring in the beginning of rainfall. The rivers of Shushuihe.
142



Suichuanjiang. Shangyoujiang, Zhangjiang. Ganjiang crossed over by the road have
stable flow with great capacity to dilute the pollutant concentration. Since there is no
centralized drinking water intake at the downstream of the bridges, the run-off from
the bridge pavement will have a very little impact on the river water quality.
(5) The Suichun and Ganzhou service areas will produce a total daily sewage and
vehicle washing waste water of 204.2-535.2 tons, which will be treated by sewage
treatment facility. After being treated, the sewage can be used to spray plants or
discharged into nearby canals, thus exerting little impact on environment.
9.3 Acoustic Environment
(1) General construction and hauling machines have relatively large impact on
people nearby the construction site (50m), and small impact beyond 100m,
particularly the construction noise at the night will impact the people' s rest and sleep.
For example. schools and hospitals and residences within 50m from the road center
(including connecting road) can have a relatively large impact from construction noise.
Therefore proper construction time schedule shall be made to avoid work at school
time and night time.
(2) In accordance with the Class IV standard limit of GB3096-93 (70dB daytime
and 55dB nighttime). the daytime noise level on both sides of the highway will be in
compliance with the standard limit in the operation period; the nighttime noise
compliant distance is 60m in the initial operation stage. and will be increased with
traffic volume, and will be 10Gm in the long term operation stage. This shows that for
ordinary residences, the daytime noise impact is relatively smaller and the nighttime
noise impact will be greater.
(3) In davtime. the Zhuhu Primary School. Mashuang High School and Qiubian
Primarv School will have a noise excess of more than 9.3dB, and max. up toI3.6dB in
the long-term operation stage, a serious impact on the school teaching. Therefore
protection measures as removal and sound barriers shall be taken. For Wuling High
School. the daytime traffic noise is exceeding by 0.8-2.6dB for Wuling High School.
However. the teaching building is a bit far away and is perpendicular to the road. the
impact on the school teaching is not great. As for Daping Olds' home. the davtime
traffic noise will be exceeding by 2.7-7.Odb and that at nighttime is 6.8-9.8dB which
shall have great noise impact: but it is very small and could be removed 200m away
from the road.
(4) Kangfucun and the Nankang Skin Clinic have an ambient noise excess of
more than 5.7-9.9dB and that at nighttime is exceeding by 9.3-12.8dB. indicating a
high impact by the road operation. Sound barriers will be built.
(5) In the initial and middle termn operation period. all the sensitive locations have
143



no noise exceedance at daytime; in the long-run operation stage. only one sensitive
location has noise excess by 1.3dB
(6) During the initial and long term operation stage, there are 37 locations with
excessive noise at night, accounting for 38.9% of the total villages. There are 12
villages with large noise excess (more than 7.0dB) at night during the long-term
operation stage Of which, Nitangcun(KI59+440), Pang' an (K228+880), Zihecun
(K257+000) will be protected by building sound barriers; the rest (mainly the first row
of houses) will be protected by installing soundproof windows.
(7) Scattered individual household within 30m from the road center will be
excessive in noise by more than 5.0 dB  those within 30-50m from the road center
will be excessive in noise by 3.0-7.0 dB; those within 50-100m from the road
center will be excessive in noise by less than 5.0dB; those beyond lOOm can meet
the standard, those beyond 150m from the road center will be approaching the base
level. Therefore, the individual households within lOOm from the road center will be
solicited to decide whether to install soundproof windows or to remove. For
individual households beyond lOOm from road center. noise monitoring will be
carried out during operation stage to decide whether to take supplementary measures.
(8) For households without noise excess but with increasing noise level, as they
are relatively far away from the road (generally more than 60m). so the existing
measures will not have good effect. Through negotiation and obtaining their agree.
noise monitoring during operation stage will be enhanced to decide whether to remove.
to install soundproof windows or to give some economic compensation.
9.4 Ambient Air
(1) Status-quo survey shows that NOx and TSP pollution are slight. with great
environmental tolerance for NOx. Most areas passed through by the highway are rural
areas. where the air quality is in natural good conditions. without large-sized fixed
pollution source..
(2) The main environmental concerns in the construction stage are pollution of
TSP. bitumen smoke from the construction site. so if the stabilized soil mixing uses
plant mixing method and the mixing plant is set away from sensitive locations and
labor protection is provided to operators: construction road and hauling road are
sprayed water and cleaned: hauling vehicles are covered by cloth. the quarry is far
trom residences. subgrade is sprayed water in filling. then the adverse impacts can be
controlled to some degree
(3) According to forecast. in the lone term operation stage. under the condition of
cateuorv D air stability. the concentrations of NOx and CO 23m from the road center
at each section will meet the Class 1I standards; and those in each sensitive location
144



will be in compliance with the Class 11 standard limit. Under unfavorable
meteorological conditions, the NOx concentration 23m from the road center with high
traffic volume and complicated landform may exceed the standard limit.
(4) CO concentration 23m from the road center meet Class II standard limit.
(5) The two tunnels of the project are all over lOOOm long, ventilation machines
will be used so to ventilate and to relieve tail gas pollution.
9.5 Social Environment
(1) The proposed expressway will play a very important role in the social
economic development in Ji' an, Ganzhou areas and the whole Jiangxi province. The
project will also promote the local areas'  tourism resources and tertiary industry
development and improve the investment environment, promoting the adjustment and
growth of the three industries.
(2) The expressway will greatly ease the traffic pressures on the existing roads
and will improve traffic environment and reduce road traffic accident.
(3) The expressway construction inevitably takes up some land and arable land.
but overall speaking. such impact is not big and can be mitigated by adjustment of
land use pattern.
(4) Proper resettlement will be carried out strictly in accordance with the local
policy concerning land acquisition and resettlement. Since rational overpasses and
underpasses have been designed. so local people' s convenience will not be impacted
much.
(5) According to the report submitted by the cultural relics administration
department, the proposed project will not cause damage to the existing cultural relics
on the ground. The owner will call the public awareness on the protection of cultural
relics: and protective measures will be taken for the underground relics discovered in
the construction stage.
9.6 Risk of Hazardous Substance Transportation
(I) Although the accident probability of Hazardous Substance Transportation is
very small. but once happened. the consequence can be serious. Owner will formulate
emergency plan to enhance its handling ability through training and management so
as to minimize pollution risk.
(2) Analysis shows that the project has a relatively strong ability to handle
accident emergency.
9.7 Public Participation
(I) The owner has taken the public opinions into full consideration in the project
145



design. such as an auxiliary bridge will be set up on both sides of the Shangyoujiang
bridge, and one interchange will be set up for each of the counties, a number of
alternative schemes has be taken for comparison and selection.
(2) As to the possible environmental issues arising from this project, the
assessment and design units have proposed corresponding protection measures such as
to remove Zhuhu primary school, to build sound barriers in Mashuang school, to
install soundproof windows etc., which have been agreed by the influenced people.
(3) Television, broadcasting, newspaper will be used to release information to the
public, and access to environmental documents and complaint telephone will be
provided to them. The World Bank Loan Project office of JPCD released the bulletin
concerning the environmental and resettlement in Nanchang Evening, Jingangshan
Daily and Ganzhou Daily dated Oct.10- 11.
(4) Public complaint shall be handled promptly through the cooperation with the
environmental protection department.
(5) Jiangxi Provincial Expressway Administration will perform an supervision and
check over the environmental protection measures specified in the EIA report for this
project in design. construction and operation stage.
9.8 Environmental Investments and Management Plan
(I) The environmental protection cost for the proposed expressway will be
I 4.96082million RMB yuan. accounting for 0.42% in the total investment.
(2) The owner has set up a resettlement office and a 3-partv coordination group
composed of design. resettlement and environmental personnel; which is responsible
for the environmental management and resettlement issues for the project:
(3) Detailed EAP has been formulated to finalize the implementation of
mitigation measures and environmental monitoring plan.
9.9 Conclusion of the Assessment
To sum up. construction and operation of the proposed project will exert some
negative impacts on ecological environment. on local people, s daily life and
schooling: however so long as the mitigation measures recommended in this EIA have
been seriouslv finalized and implemented, the negative impacts will be under control
and reduced to an acceptable minimum. The alignment design is reasonable with
considerable social economic benefits. Therefore this EIA states that the proposed
expressway is feasible.

Annex I
Overview of the Assessment Unit and Staff Member
Research Institute Of Highway (RIOH) is the largest and comprehensive national
highway research . experiment and technical development base under the direct
leadership of the MOC, holding class A Certificates for EIA issued by NEPA.
Environmental Engineering Office of RIH is mainly engaged in environment
impact assessment (EIA) of highway and independent bridges; environment
engineering design, planting design and basic environmental research concerning
construction and communications. It now owns 20 specialists in the fields of highway
engineering, automobile engineering, environment engineering. chemical analysis,
garden planting, biochemical engineering., of whom, 10 persons have high-level
professional titles and 6 have middle-level professional titles. Up to the present, we
have carried out EIA for about 100 freeways and independent bridges. taken charge
of the compiling of Environmental Impact Assessment Specifications for Highway
Construction Projects promulgated by the MOC. Having good theoretic fundamentals
and hands-on experience. the Environmental Engineering Office also has the EIA
working experience for the projects financed by the World Bank and the Asia
Development Bank. In addition to this. it undertook the environmental design of
freeway sound barrier. sewage treatment, planting and construction work.
The following is an outline of the assessment personnel for this project:
Shen Yi. male, born in 1962. graduated from Huatong Institute of Water
Conservancy and Electric Power. He is associate research fellow and the depute
director of Environmental Engineering Office.. in charge of the coordination with the
Owner and design unit in this project
Yan Xiaolin, male, born in 1969, M.S. graduated from Research Institute of
Environmental Science of Beijing Normal University. He is an associate research
fellow. in charge of the EIA (the main line) compiling and the acoustic assessment in
this project
Li Xivun. female. born in 1941, graduated from Fudan University. senior engineer.
in charge of the EAP compiling and the ambient assessment in this project
Wang fang. female. born in 1957. graduated from Electronic engineering.,
assistant engineer. in charge of the social environment assessment in this project
Dong Bochang. male. born in 1974. M.S graduated from  Environmental
Engineering of Jilin University. assistant research fellow, in charge of ecological
environment and soil erosion assessment in this project
Fan Qinchun. female. born in 1974. graduated from Beijing Industrial University.
engineer. in charge of the water environment assessment in this project
